 - name: "Aether Compass"
   description: "This plugin detects certain objects/NPCs such as Aether Currents nearby and shows where they are by various ways, e.g. pointing to their locations on screen and notifying you in Chat.<br>Currently detects:<br>	- Aether Currents<br>	- Eureka Elementals (by apetih)<br>	- Mob Hunt Elite Marks<br>	- Gathering Points<br>	- [Experimental] Island Sanctuary Gathering Objects and Animals<br>	- [Experimental] Quest-related NPCs/Objects <br>Note: Because most objects/NPCs are not loaded when they are too faraway or when there are too many entities nearby (such as too many player characters), they will not be detected in this case.<br>Icon by Lumas Arkfrost"
   punchline: "Compasses that detect and mark certain nearby objects/NPCs"

 - name: "Fashion Report Calculator / Dye Finder"
   description: "This is the new and improved Fashion Report System. This plugin will allow you to open a window that will show you what your fashion report status is vs the current week's theme.<br>There are a few parts to this. Since the only way to get Fashion Report for the week to my knowledge is speaking to Masked Rose after Tuesdays reset, this plugin takes the first person who does talk to him and updates everyone else. So only one person per week needs to speak to Masked Rose.<br>You can click on a theme and pull all the known items for that theme for that specific slot. You also get a very detailed breakdown of how much points you are getting based on what you are currently wearing.<br>The plugin also stores the attempts of those using the mod (just the data from fashioncheck, no user information) so that we can figure out the dyes faster and share information faster. The information in this table is wiped every week since once we discover the dyes, it is useless.<br>I still have more upgrades to do, including adding a dye window and the window that will help calculate the weekly dyes. I already have an idea of how I want to write them, so it shouldn't take me too long. If you have suggestions on how I can upgrade this, please share with me on github!<br>Credit for the program goes to it's original creator, WillWolf76, who wrote this for me originally.<br>When this plugin updates the database, it also updates my Discord Bot which you can set up to post fashion report each week. It's set to update on Tuesdays and Fridays (week start and dye information added). Link to add the Discord Bot is in the about section."
   punchline: "Know your Fashion Report points on the spot and help crowdsource new items and dyes!"

 - name: "XIVJitterFix"
   description: "With the release of 7.0 SquareEnix has implemented several temporal antialiasing solutions. However they all have a severe bug that affects image quality significantly.<br>This plugin will restore using jitter when talking to NPCs or in cutscenes and gpose. Jitter (not noticeable micromovements of the camera) is necessary for temporal antialiasing solutions (DLSS, DLAA, TSCMAA+jitter) to work properly.<br>For some reason, SquareEnix decided we don't need jitter during the time where the game benefits from using it the most."
